#Adventurers
estate_adventurers_organization_chronicler_grants = {
	icon = privilege_promote_maratha_nobility
	max_absolutism = -5
	conditional_modifier = { trigger = { has_absolutism_reduction_for_estate_privileges = yes } modifier = { max_absolutism = 1 } }
	conditional_modifier = { #Magisterium imperial incident
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = enforced_independence_of_chroniclers_flag
		}
		modifier = {
			embracement_cost = -0.25
			adm_tech_cost_modifier = -0.075
			mages_influence_modifier = -0.10
		}
	}
	loyalty = 0.05
	influence = 0.05
	land_share = 5
	is_valid = {
		NOT = { has_adventurers_special_organization_privilege = yes }
	}
	can_select = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_adventurers_organization_privilege = yes }
			NOT = {
				estate_influence = {
					estate = estate_adventurers
					influence = 25
				}
			}
			estate_loyalty = {
				estate = estate_adventurers
				loyalty = 30
			}

			if = {
				limit = {
					estate_loyalty = {
						estate = estate_adventurers
						loyalty = 60
					}
				}
				mil_power = 100
				stability = 1
			}
			else = {
				mil_power = 200
				stability = 2
			}
		}
		has_discovered = 8 #Anbenncost
	}
	can_revoke = {
		always = no
	}
	on_granted = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_adventurers_organization_privilege = yes
				NOT = { has_estate_privilege = estate_adventurers_organization_chronicler_grants }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					estate_loyalty = {
						estate = estate_adventurers
						loyalty = 60
					}
				}
				add_mil_power = -100
				add_stability = -1
			}
			else = {
				add_stability = -2
				add_mil_power = -200
			}
			custom_tooltip = estate_adventurers_organization_cost_tooltip
			custom_tooltip = estate_adventurers_organization_revoke_tooltip
			clear_adventurers_organization_effect = yes
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { is_year = 1445 } }
				take_estate_land_share_massive = { estate = estate_adventurers }
			}
		}
	}
	penalties = {
		mercenary_manpower = -0.2
	}
	benefits = {
		global_institution_spread = 0.2
		innovativeness_gain = 0.25
	}
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 10
			any_known_country = {
				institution_difference = {
					who = ROOT
					value = 2
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

estate_adventurers_contain_dangerous_artefacts = {
	icon = privilege_monopoly_of_goods_precursor_relics
	loyalty = 0.05
	land_share = 5
	is_valid = {
		has_estate_privilege = estate_adventurers_organization_scp_bureau
		has_country_flag = scp_bureau_containment_unlocked
		any_owned_province = { trade_goods = precursor_relics }
	}
	can_select = {
		custom_trigger_tooltip = {
			tooltip = unavailable_during_revolution_disaster
			NOT = { has_disaster = revolution }
			NOT = {
				has_disaster_progress = {
					disaster = revolution
					value = 1
				}
			}
		}
		custom_trigger_tooltip = {
			tooltip = JY_LF_not_trading #Anbennar
			NOT = { has_country_modifier = JY_LF_recent_trade }
		}
	}
	on_granted = { custom_tooltip = estate_containment_gain_land_tt }
	on_granted_province = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				trade_goods = precursor_relics
			}
			add_province_modifier = { name = H33_containment_mod duration = -1 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_province_modifier = H33_containment_mod }
			remove_province_modifier = H33_containment_mod
		}
	}
	on_revoked = { custom_tooltip = H33_revoke_containment_tt }
	on_revoked_province = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_province_modifier = H33_containment_mod }
			remove_province_modifier = H33_containment_mod
		}
	}
	on_invalid = { custom_tooltip = H33_revoke_containment_tt }
	on_invalid_province = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_province_modifier = H33_containment_mod }
			remove_province_modifier = H33_containment_mod
		}
	}
	penalties = {
	}
	benefits = {
	}
	cooldown_years = 10
	modifier_by_land_ownership = {
		global_unrest = -4
		global_spy_defence = 0.4
		stability_cost_modifier = -0.2
	}
	# mechanics = {
	# 	exempt_from_seize_land
	# }
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 5
	}
}

estate_adventurers_ennoblement_of_adventurers = {
	icon = privilege_royal_authority
	max_absolutism = -5
	conditional_modifier = { trigger = { has_absolutism_reduction_for_estate_privileges = yes } modifier = { max_absolutism = 1 } }
	loyalty = 0.05
	land_share = 5
	influence = 0.05
	is_valid = { NOT = { OR = { religion = gods_of_the_taychend religion = oren_nayiru } } NOT = { has_country_flag = estate_adventurers_ennoblement_of_adventurers_invalid } }
	can_select = {
		OR = {
			has_estate = estate_nobles
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = no_nobles_ennoblement_of_adventurers_tt
				has_country_flag = no_nobles_ennoblement_of_adventurers
			}
		}
	}
	on_granted = {
	}
	penalties = {
		nobles_loyalty_modifier = -0.05
	}
	benefits = {
		governing_capacity = 100
	}
	conditional_modifier = {		#part of arbaran's mission tree
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = arbaran_improved_ennoblement_privilege
		}
		modifier = {
			mercenary_cost = -0.20
			mercenary_discipline = 0.05
		}
	}
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 5
		modifier = {
			factor = 5
			tag = A46			#ennoblement of adventurers is a very Arbarani thing to do, it's part of their national ideas, also it will help the AI complete a mission
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.4
			num_of_territories = 5
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			num_of_territories = 10
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			num_of_territories = 15
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			OR = {
				NOT = { crown_land_share = 25 }
				estate_influence = {
					estate = estate_adventurers
					influence = 75
				}
			}
			NOT = { has_estate_privilege = estate_adventurers_ennoblement_of_adventurers }
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 3
			OR = {
				AND = {
					governing_capacity_percentage = 0.9
					NOT = { has_estate_privilege = estate_adventurers_ennoblement_of_adventurers }
				}
				#The trigger below should make sure that the AI actually keeps this privilege when enacting it early game
				AND = {
					governing_capacity_percentage = 0.6
					has_estate_privilege = estate_adventurers_ennoblement_of_adventurers
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			NOT = { governing_capacity_percentage = 0.5 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			OR = {
				NOT = { crown_land_share = 40 }
				AND = {
					is_absolutism_active = yes
					NOT = { crown_land_share = 60 }
				}
			}
			NOT = { has_estate_privilege = estate_adventurers_ennoblement_of_adventurers }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			OR = {
				NOT = { crown_land_share = 30 }
				AND = {
					is_absolutism_active = yes
					NOT = { crown_land_share = 50 }
				}
			}
			NOT = { has_estate_privilege = estate_adventurers_ennoblement_of_adventurers }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			is_absolutism_active = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			NOT = {
				estate_loyalty = {
					estate = estate_nobles
					loyalty = 25
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

estate_adventurers_cavern_exploration_initiative = {
	icon = privilege_grant_new_world_charter
	max_absolutism = -5
	conditional_modifier = { trigger = { has_absolutism_reduction_for_estate_privileges = yes } modifier = { max_absolutism = 1 } }
	loyalty = 0.05
	influence = 0.05
	is_valid = {
		OR = {
			num_of_colonists = 1
			num_of_colonies = 1
		}
		capital_scope = {
			continent = serpentspine
		}
		NOT = {
			colony = 1
		}
	}
	penalties = {
		global_tax_modifier = -0.05
	}
	benefits = {
		global_colonial_growth = 10
		colonist_placement_chance = 0.05
	}
	on_granted = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_dlc = "Domination" }
			enable_estate_action = {
				estate_action = CAVERN_EXPLORATION_INITIATIVE_ADVENTURERS
			}
		}
		else = {
			custom_tooltip = has_no_effects_on_granted
		}
	}
	on_invalid = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_dlc = "Domination" }
			disable_estate_action = {
				estate_action = CAVERN_EXPLORATION_INITIATIVE_ADVENTURERS
			}
		}
		else = {
			hidden_effect = {
				disable_estate_action = {
					estate_action = CAVERN_EXPLORATION_INITIATIVE_ADVENTURERS
				}
			}
		}
	}
	on_revoked = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_dlc = "Domination" }
			disable_estate_action = {
				estate_action = CAVERN_EXPLORATION_INITIATIVE_ADVENTURERS
			}
		}
		else = {
			hidden_effect = {
				disable_estate_action = {
					estate_action = CAVERN_EXPLORATION_INITIATIVE_ADVENTURERS
				}
			}
		}
	}
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 10
			AND = {
				capital_scope = {
					continent = serpentspine
				}
				any_owned_province = {
					has_empty_adjacent_province = yes
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			is_absolutism_active = yes
		}
	}
}

estate_adventurers_monopoly_of_slaves = {
	icon = privilege_monopoly_of_goods_slaves
	max_absolutism = -10
	conditional_modifier = { trigger = { has_absolutism_reduction_for_estate_privileges = yes } modifier = { max_absolutism = 2 } }
	loyalty = 0.1
	is_valid = {
		has_dlc = "Emperor"
		slaves = 1
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = no_longer_monstrous
			tag = R38
		}
	}
	can_select = {
		custom_trigger_tooltip = {
			tooltip = unavailable_during_revolution_disaster
			NOT = { has_disaster = revolution }
			NOT = {
				has_disaster_progress = {
					disaster = revolution
					value = 1
				}
			}
		}
		custom_trigger_tooltip = {
			tooltip = JY_LF_not_trading #Anbennar
			NOT = { has_country_modifier = JY_LF_recent_trade }
		}
	}
	can_revoke = { hidden_trigger = { NOT = { has_global_flag = adventurers_remove_slaves } } }
	on_granted = {
		add_mercantilism = 1
		add_years_of_owned_provinces_production_income = {
			years = 8
			trigger = {
				trade_goods = slaves
			}
			custom_tooltip = MONOPOLY_INCOME_SLAVES_DESC
		}
		custom_tooltip = estate_church_monopoly_of_slaves_effect_tooltip

	}
	on_granted_province = {
		if = {
			limit = { trade_goods = slaves }
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = estate_adventurers_monopoly_of_slaves_mod
				duration = -1
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_province_modifier = estate_adventurers_monopoly_of_slaves_mod }
			remove_province_modifier = estate_adventurers_monopoly_of_slaves_mod
		}
	}

	on_revoked = {
		custom_tooltip = estate_church_monopoly_of_slaves_revoke_tooltip
	}
	on_revoked_province = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_province_modifier = estate_adventurers_monopoly_of_slaves_mod }
			remove_province_modifier = estate_adventurers_monopoly_of_slaves_mod
		}
	}
	on_invalid = {
		custom_tooltip = estate_church_monopoly_of_slaves_revoke_tooltip
	}
	on_invalid_province = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_province_modifier = estate_adventurers_monopoly_of_slaves_mod }
			remove_province_modifier = estate_adventurers_monopoly_of_slaves_mod
		}
	}
	penalties = {
	}
	benefits = {
	}
	cooldown_years = 10
	on_cooldown_expires = {
		country_event = { id = monopoly_privileges.13 }
	}
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 0
	}
}

	}

		# custom_tooltip = unlock_merc_yidabs_vanguard_tt
		unlock_merc_company = {
			merc_company = merc_yidabs_vanguard
			free_merc = yes # Only include this line if "elite" merc that costs no professionalism
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = I98_yidab_merc
		}
	}

	on_revoked = {
		hidden_effect = {
			clr_country_flag = I98_yidab_merc
		}
		random_hired_mercenary_company = {
			limit = {
				home_province = {
					province_id = 4070
				}
			}
			disband_mercenary_company = THIS
		}
		add_estate_loyalty = {
			estate = estate_adventurers
			loyalty = 10
		}
	}

	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 5
	}
}

estate_adventurers_bellacaire_sappers = {
	icon = privilege_artillery
	loyalty = 0
	influence = 0.1
	is_valid = {
		has_country_flag = guardsmen_unlocked
		is_or_was_tag = { tag = B59 } #Pashaine
	}
	
	can_select = {
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = guardsmen_privilege_no_limit } }
			NOT = {
				has_estate_privilege = estate_adventurers_napesbay_squadron
				has_estate_privilege = estate_adventurers_menibor_vanguard
				has_estate_privilege = estate_adventurers_bluehart_finest
			}
		}
		else = { always = yes }
	}

	can_revoke = { always = yes }

	penalties = {
		allowed_rev_guard_fraction = -0.1
	}

	benefits = {
		artillery_barrage_cost = -0.5
	}

	conditional_modifier = {
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = guardsmen_privilege_no_limit
		}
		modifier = { land_morale = 0.025 }
	}
}

#Aelantir-Cannor Interaction
estate_adventurers_help_expedition_1 = {
	icon = privilege_monopoly_of_goods_iron
	max_absolutism = -10
	conditional_modifier = { trigger = { has_absolutism_reduction_for_estate_privileges = yes } modifier = { max_absolutism = 2 } }
	loyalty = -0.05
	influence = 0.1
	is_valid = {
		has_reform = state_sponsored_aelantiri_expedition
		NOT = {
			check_variable = {
   				which = send_help_adventurers
    			value = 15
			}
		}
	}
	can_select = {
		always = yes
	}
	can_revoke = {
		always = no
	}
	on_granted = {
		add_adm_power = 25
		add_dip_power = 25
		add_mil_power = 25
		custom_tooltip = expedition_help_privilege_upgrade_tt
		if = {
			limit = { cannor_sponsor_of_aelant_exp_vg = yes }
			G97 = {
				estate_help_expedition_effect = {
					modifier = aelantir_exp_cannorian_adventurers
					devtype = random_development
				}
			}
		}
		# if = {
		# 	limit = { cannor_sponsor_of_aelant_exp_csltc = yes }
		# 	G98 = {
		# 		estate_help_expedition_effect = {
		# 			modifier = aelantir_exp_cannorian_adventurers
		# 			devtype = random_development
		# 		}
		# 	}
		# }
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_or_was_tag = { tag = A95 }
			}
			H37 = {
				estate_help_expedition_effect = {
					modifier = aelantir_exp_cannorian_adventurers
					devtype = random_development
				}
			}
		}
	}
	penalties = {
		global_tax_modifier = -0.1
		mercenary_manpower = -0.25
	}
	benefits = {
	}
	influence_scaled_conditional_modifier = {
		trigger = { always = yes }
		modifier = { mercenary_manpower = -0.25 }
	}

	cooldown_years = 10
	on_cooldown_expires = {
		if = {
			limit = { 
				NOT = {
					check_variable = {
   						which = send_help_adventurers
    					value = 14
					}
				}
			}
			country_event = { id = aelantir_cannor_interaction.406 }
		}
		else = {
			country_event = { id = aelantir_cannor_interaction.407 }
		}
	}
	on_revoked = {
		ael_cannor_interactions_on_remove = { modifier = aelantir_exp_cannorian_adventurers }
	}
	on_invalid = {
		ael_cannor_interactions_on_remove = { modifier = aelantir_exp_cannorian_adventurers }
	}
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 100
	}
}

		}

				}

		trigger = { always = yes }
		modifier = { mercenary_manpower = -0.25 }
	}
	conditional_modifier = {
		trigger = {  has_estate = estate_artificers }
		modifier = { artificers_capacity = 5 }
	}
	conditional_modifier = {
		trigger = { 
			NOT = { has_estate = estate_artificers }
			has_estate = estate_mages
		}
		modifier = { all_power_cost = -0.025 }
	}
	on_revoked = {
		ael_cannor_interactions_on_remove = { modifier = aelantir_exp_cannorian_adventurers }
	}
	on_invalid = {
		ael_cannor_interactions_on_remove = { modifier = aelantir_exp_cannorian_adventurers }
	}
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 100
	}
}

#Monstrous Tribes
estate_monstrous_tribes_land_rights = {
	icon = privilege_grant_autonomy
	land_share = 5
	max_absolutism = -5
	conditional_modifier = { trigger = { has_absolutism_reduction_for_estate_privileges = yes } modifier = { max_absolutism = 1 } }
	loyalty = 0.05
	influence = 0.05
	can_select = {
	}
	on_granted = {
	}
	penalties = {
	}
	benefits = {
		governing_capacity = 100
	}
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 5
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.4
			num_of_territories = 5
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			num_of_territories = 10
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			num_of_territories = 15
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			OR = {
				NOT = { crown_land_share = 25 }
				estate_influence = {
					estate = estate_monstrous_tribes
					influence = 75
				}
			}
			NOT = { has_estate_privilege = estate_monstrous_tribes_land_rights }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 3
			OR = {
				AND = {
					governing_capacity_percentage = 0.9
					NOT = { has_estate_privilege = estate_monstrous_tribes_land_rights }
				}
				#The trigger below should make sure that the AI actually keeps this privilege when enacting it early game
				AND = {
					governing_capacity_percentage = 0.6
					has_estate_privilege = estate_monstrous_tribes_land_rights
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			NOT = { governing_capacity_percentage = 0.5 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			OR = {
				NOT = { crown_land_share = 40 }
				AND = {
					is_absolutism_active = yes
					NOT = { crown_land_share = 60 }
				}
			}
			NOT = { has_estate_privilege = estate_monstrous_tribes_land_rights }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			OR = {
				NOT = { crown_land_share = 30 }
				AND = {
					is_absolutism_active = yes
					NOT = { crown_land_share = 50 }
				}
			}
			NOT = { has_estate_privilege = estate_monstrous_tribes_land_rights }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			is_absolutism_active = yes
		}
	}
}

	max_absolutism = -5

	}
	can_select = {

			tooltip = take_primary_cult_decision_tt2

				has_country_flag = has_selected_a_primary_cult
			}
		}
		NOT = { has_estate_privilege = estate_monstrous_tribes_flexible_cults }
		NOT = { has_estate_privilege = estate_monstrous_tribes_heir_shrine }
	}
	can_revoke = {
		custom_trigger_tooltip = {
			tooltip = remove_primary_cult_decision_tt
			had_country_flag = {
				flag = has_selected_a_primary_cult
				days = 3600
			}
		}
	}
	on_granted = {
		enable_primary_cult = yes
	}
	on_revoked = {
		disable_primary_cult = yes
		add_stability = -2
	}
	on_invalid = {
		disable_primary_cult = yes
	}
	penalties = {
	}
	benefits = {
		# duplicate, selecting a primary cult already gives back the stab
		# no_stability_loss_on_monarch_death = yes
	}
#	conditional_modifier = {
#		trigger = { has_government_attribute = no_influence_from_fetishist_privileges }
#		modifier = {
#			monstrous_tribes_influence_modifier = -0.25
#		}
#	}
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 1000

#		}
	}

#Church

estate_church_guaranteed_autonomy = {
	icon = privilege_grant_autonomy
	max_absolutism = -5
	conditional_modifier = { trigger = { has_absolutism_reduction_for_estate_privileges = yes } modifier = { max_absolutism = 1 } }
	influence = 0.05
	loyalty = -0.05
	is_valid = {
		OR = {
			tag = Y63 # Anbennar Temporary for Verkal Ozovar, to stop them spreading AW in Haless.
			religion_group = raheni
		}
		NOT = { capital_scope = { superregion = rahen_superregion } }
		any_owned_province = {
			religion_group = halessi
		}
	}
	can_select = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = rending_started_country }
			any_owned_province = {
				OR = {
					religion = accretive_path
					religion = transmutative_path
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			any_owned_province = {
				OR = {
					religion = accretive_path
					religion = transmutative_path
					religion = mystic_accord
				}
			}
		}
	}
	on_granted = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = rending_started_country }
			custom_tooltip = estate_church_guaranteed_autonomy_effect_tooltip2
		}
		else = { custom_tooltip = estate_church_guaranteed_autonomy_effect_tooltip }
	}
	on_granted_province = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					religion = accretive_path
					religion = transmutative_path
					AND = {
						religion = mystic_accord
						NOT = { owner = { has_country_flag = rending_started_country } }
					}
				}
			}
			add_province_modifier = { name = estate_church_guaranteed_autonomy_mod duration = -1 }
		}
		else = {
			remove_province_modifier = estate_church_guaranteed_autonomy_mod
		}
	}
	on_revoked = {
		custom_tooltip = estate_church_guaranteed_autonomy_revoke_effect_tooltip
	}
	on_revoked_province = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_modifier = estate_church_guaranteed_autonomy_mod
			}
			remove_province_modifier = estate_church_guaranteed_autonomy_mod
		}
	}
	on_invalid = {
		custom_tooltip = estate_church_guaranteed_autonomy_revoke_effect_tooltip
	}
	on_invalid_province = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_modifier = estate_church_guaranteed_autonomy_mod
			}
			remove_province_modifier = estate_church_guaranteed_autonomy_mod
		}
	}
	penalties = {
	}
	benefits = {
	}
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 1000
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			religious_unity = 1.0
			NOT = { has_estate_privilege = estate_church_guaranteed_autonomy }
		}
		modifier = { # Anbennar
			factor = 0
			OR = {
				tag = Y65	# Arawkelin
				tag = Y69	# Brenulan
				# Sarisung vassals:
				tag = R15	# Nundujisbid
				tag = R37	# Kethur
				tag = R59	# Khappur
				tag = R60	# Sarkhani
			}
		}
	}
}

estate_nobles_tribes_tame_the_frontier_privilege = {
	icon = privilege_grant_new_world_charter
	influence = 0.05
	loyalty = 0.05
	max_absolutism = 0
	is_valid = {
		capital_scope = { superregion = gerudia_superregion }
		culture_native_to_gerudia_superregion = yes
	}
	can_select = {
		adm_tech = 5
	}
	can_revoke = {
		always = yes
	}
	on_granted = {
		custom_tooltip = estate_nobles_tribes_tame_the_frontier_dt
		custom_tooltip = estate_nobles_tribes_tame_the_frontier_nt
		tooltip = {
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = estate_tame_the_frontier_new_colony_mod
				duration = 18250 #50 years
			}
		}
		
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = temporary_colonist
			duration = -1
		}
		custom_tooltip = estate_nobles_tribes_tame_the_frontier_ct
	}
	on_granted_province = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_colony = yes
				OR = {
					region = yyl_moista_region
					region = northern_pass_region
					superregion = gerudia_superregion
				}
			}
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = estate_tame_the_frontier_discount_mod
				duration = -1
			}
		}
		else = {
			remove_province_modifier = estate_tame_the_frontier_discount_mod
		}
	}
	on_revoked_province = {
		remove_province_modifier = estate_tame_the_frontier_discount_mod
	}
	on_revoked = {
		remove_temporary_colonist = yes
	}
	penalties = {
		range = -0.25
	}
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 5 #>10 take, <5 revoke
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			capital_scope = { superregion = gerudia_superregion }
			culture_native_to_gerudia_superregion = yes
			adm_tech = 5
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			capital_scope = { superregion = gerudia_superregion }
			culture_native_to_gerudia_superregion = yes
			has_estate_privilege = estate_nobles_tribes_tame_the_frontier_privilege
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.2
			has_idea_group = exploration_ideas
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			has_idea_group = expansion_ideas
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			NOT = { 
				any_owned_province = { 
					OR = {
						superregion = gerudia_superregion
						region = yyl_moista_region
						region = northern_pass_region
					}
					OR = {
						has_empty_adjacent_province = yes 
						is_colony = yes
					}
				} 
			}
		}
	}
}

#khugdihr
estate_church_khug_ancestral_worshippers = {
	icon = privilege_religious_diplomats
	influence = 0.2
	is_valid = { has_country_flag = ancestral_worshippers_unlocked }
	benefits = { tolerance_heathen = 2 }
	on_granted = {
		custom_tooltip = khug_religion_opinion_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = khug_religious_opinion
			every_known_country = {
				limit = {
					religion = ancestor_worship
					NOT = {
						has_opinion_modifier = {
							who = ROOT
							modifier = khug_religion
						}
					}
				}
				add_opinion = {
					who = ROOT
					modifier = khug_religion
				}
				reverse_add_opinion = {
					who = ROOT
					modifier = khug_religion
				}
			}
		}
	}
	on_revoked = {
		custom_tooltip = khug_remove_religion_opinion_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			clr_country_flag = khug_religious_opinion
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					AND = {
						has_opinion_modifier = {
							who = ROOT
							modifier = khug_religion
						}
						religion = ancestor_worship
					}
				}
				remove_opinion = {
					who = ROOT
					modifier = khug_religion
				}
				reverse_remove_opinion = {
					who = ROOT
					modifier = khug_religion
				}
			}
		}
	}
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 1
	}
}

xhazobkult_flesh_of_flesh = {
	icon = privilege_seek_support_of_clergy
	max_absolutism = -5
	conditional_modifier = { trigger = { has_country_flag = estate_church_no_absolutism_cost } modifier = { max_absolutism = 5 } }
	conditional_modifier = { trigger = { has_absolutism_reduction_for_estate_privileges = yes NOT = { has_country_flag = estate_church_no_absolutism_cost } } modifier = { max_absolutism = 1 } }
	influence = 0.05
	loyalty = 0.05
	is_valid = {
		religion = xhazobkult
		has_ruler_flag = undergoing_xhazob_ritual
		NOT = { has_country_flag = zokka_zokka_heir_of_zokka_flag }
	}
	can_select = {
		is_summoning_xhazob_trigger = yes
		OR = {
			government = tribal
			government = monarchy
		}
	}
	on_revoked = {
		reduce_stability_or_adm_power = yes
	}
	on_granted = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_heir = yes }
			kill_heir = { allow_new_heir = no }
		}
		reduce_stability_or_adm_power = yes
	}
	penalties = {
		heir_chance = -1
		stability_cost_modifier = 0.75
	}
	benefits = {
		yearly_patriarch_authority = 0.01
	}
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 5
	}
}

estate_church_protected_burials = {
	icon = privilege_build_jain_temple
	max_absolutism = -5
	conditional_modifier = { trigger = { has_country_flag = estate_church_no_absolutism_cost } modifier = { max_absolutism = 5 } }
	conditional_modifier = { trigger = { has_absolutism_reduction_for_estate_privileges = yes NOT = { has_country_flag = estate_church_no_absolutism_cost } } modifier = { max_absolutism = 1 } }
	loyalty = 0.05
	influence = 0.05
	is_valid = {
	}
	penalties = {
		global_manpower_modifier = -0.10
	}
	benefits = {
		prestige = 0.5
	}
	on_granted = {
		custom_tooltip = reduced_aw_ghouls_tt
		if = {
			limit = { prestige = 50 }
			add_prestige = 5
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { prestige = 0 }
			add_prestige = 10
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { prestige = -25 }
			add_prestige = 15
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { prestige = -50 }
			add_prestige = 20
		}
		else = {
			add_prestige = 25
		}
	}
	on_revoked = {
		custom_tooltip = reduced_aw_ghouls_tt
	}
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 0
	}
}

			OR = {
				has_province_modifier = temple_complex
				has_province_modifier = damaged_temple_complex
				has_province_modifier = derelict_temple_complex
				has_province_modifier = ruined_temple_complex
			}
		}
	}
	can_select = {
		any_owned_province = {
			OR = {
				has_province_modifier = temple_complex
				has_province_modifier = damaged_temple_complex
				has_province_modifier = derelict_temple_complex
				has_province_modifier = ruined_temple_complex
			}
		}
	}
	on_granted = {
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = spirits.500 }
		}
		custom_tooltip = will_begin_temple_quest_preparations_tooltip
	}
	penalties = {
	}
	benefits = {
		global_tax_modifier = 0.1		#The adventurers are paying you for Temple Quest Licenses
	}
	conditional_modifier = {
		trigger = {
			religion = high_philosophy
		}
		modifier = {
			church_loyalty_modifier = -0.1
			tolerance_own = -1
		}
	}
	cooldown_years = 10
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 0
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			religion = high_philosophy
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 5
			capital_scope = {
				NOT = {
					OR = {
						superregion = yanshen_superregion
						superregion = rahen_superregion
						superregion = vimdatrong_superregion
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

estate_church_balgarsmiths_mining = {
	icon = privilege_build_jain_temple
	max_absolutism = -5
	conditional_modifier = { trigger = { has_country_flag = estate_church_no_absolutism_cost } modifier = { max_absolutism = 5 } }
	conditional_modifier = { trigger = { has_absolutism_reduction_for_estate_privileges = yes NOT = { has_country_flag = estate_church_no_absolutism_cost } } modifier = { max_absolutism = 1 } }
	loyalty = 0.05
	influence = 0.1
	is_valid = {
		tag = Z36
		has_country_flag = has_balgarsmiths
	}
	can_select = {
		tag = Z36
		has_country_flag = has_balgarsmiths
	}
	on_granted = {
		custom_tooltip = estate_church_balgarsmiths_mining_tooltip
		hidden_effect = {
		 	every_owned_province = {
		 		limit = {
		 			trade_goods = iron
					trade_goods = copper
		 		}
		 		add_province_modifier = {
		 			name = Z36_balgarsmiths_production_bonus
		 			duration = -1
		 		}
		 	}
		 }
	}

	can_revoke = {
		always = yes
	}

	on_granted_province = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					trade_goods = copper
					trade_goods = iron
				}
			}
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = Z36_balgarsmiths_production_bonus
				duration = -1
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_modifier = Z36_balgarsmiths_production_bonus
			}
			remove_province_modifier = Z36_balgarsmiths_production_bonus
		}
	}
	on_revoked = {
		custom_tooltip = estate_church_balgarsmiths_mining_revoke_tooltip
	}
	on_revoked_province = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_modifier = Z36_balgarsmiths_production_bonus
			}
			remove_province_modifier = Z36_balgarsmiths_production_bonus
		}
	}
	on_invalid = {
		custom_tooltip = estate_church_balgarsmiths_mining_revoke_tooltip
	}
	on_invalid_province = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_modifier = Z36_balgarsmiths_production_bonus
			}
			remove_province_modifier = Z36_balgarsmiths_production_bonus
		}
	}
	penalties = {
	}
	benefits = {
	}
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 0
	}
}

#Barumand
estate_nobility_permanent_embassies = {
    icon = privilege_promote_maratha_nobility
    max_absolutism = -10
	conditional_modifier = { trigger = { has_absolutism_reduction_for_estate_privileges = yes } modifier = { max_absolutism = 2 } }
    loyalty = 0.20
    influence = 0.10
    is_valid = {
        has_country_flag = barumand_embassy_privilege
    }
    can_revoke = {
        always = yes
    }

    on_granted = {
        custom_tooltip = barumand_increase_subject_opinion_tt
        hidden_effect = {
            every_subject_country = {
                limit = {
                    NOT = {
                        has_opinion_modifier = {
                            who = ROOT
                            modifier = barumand_increase_subject_opinion
                        }
                    }
                }
                add_opinion = {
                    who = ROOT
                    modifier = barumand_increase_subject_opinion
                }
            }
        }
    }
	on_revoked = {
        custom_tooltip = barumand_remove_increase_subject_opinion_tt
        hidden_effect = {
            every_subject_country = {
                limit = {
                    has_opinion_modifier = {
                        who = ROOT
                        modifier = barumand_increase_subject_opinion
                    }
                }
                remove_opinion = {
                    who = ROOT
                    modifier = barumand_increase_subject_opinion
                }
            }
        }
    }

    on_invalid = {
        custom_tooltip = barumand_remove_increase_subject_opinion_tt
        hidden_effect = {
            every_subject_country = {
                limit = {
                    has_opinion_modifier = {
                        who = ROOT
                        modifier = barumand_increase_subject_opinion
                    }
                }
                remove_opinion = {
                    who = ROOT
                    modifier = barumand_increase_subject_opinion
                }
            }
        }
    }

    benefits = {
        improve_relation_modifier = 0.1
    }
	ai_will_do = { factor = 1 }
}

#Freemarches Rudmen
estate_burghers_rudmen_traders = {
	icon = privilege_new_world_mission
	max_absolutism = -5
	conditional_modifier = { trigger = { has_absolutism_reduction_for_estate_privileges = yes } modifier = { max_absolutism = 1 } }
	influence = 0.05
	loyalty = 0.1
	is_valid = {
		tag = H51
		has_country_flag = freemarches_rudmen_traders_unlocked 
		
		has_dlc = "Emperor"
		any_owned_province = {
			trade_goods = fur
		}
	}

	can_revoke = {
		always = yes
	}
	
	on_granted = {
		custom_tooltip = estate_burghers_rudmen_traders_tooltip
		hidden_effect = {
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = fur
				}
				add_province_modifier = {
					name = H51_rudmen_traders_production_bonus
					duration = -1
				}
			}
			add_mercantilism = -2
	 	}
	}
	on_granted_province = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				trade_goods = fur
			}
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = H51_rudmen_traders_production_bonus
				duration = -1
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_modifier = H51_rudmen_traders_production_bonus
			}
			remove_province_modifier = H51_rudmen_traders_production_bonus
		}
	}
	on_revoked = {
		custom_tooltip = estate_burghers_rudmen_traders_revoke_tooltip
	}
	on_revoked_province = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_modifier = H51_rudmen_traders_production_bonus
			}
			remove_province_modifier = H51_rudmen_traders_production_bonus
		}
	}
	on_invalid = {
		custom_tooltip = estate_burghers_rudmen_traders_revoke_tooltip
	}
	on_invalid_province = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_modifier = H51_rudmen_traders_production_bonus
			}
			remove_province_modifier = H51_rudmen_traders_production_bonus
		}
	}
	penalties = {
	}
	benefits = {
	}
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 1
	}
}

estate_nobles_orldhum_ostentatious_overseers = {
	icon = privilege_monopoly_of_goods_slaves
	max_absolutism = -5
	conditional_modifier = { trigger = { has_absolutism_reduction_for_estate_privileges = yes } modifier = { max_absolutism = 1 } }
	loyalty = 0.05
	influence = 0.1
	is_valid = {
		has_country_flag = orldhum_ostentatious_overseers
	}
	can_select = {
		any_owned_province = {
			trade_goods = slaves
		}
		NOT = { has_estate_privilege = estate_church_monopoly_of_slaves }
	}
	on_granted = {
		custom_tooltip = estate_nobles_orldhum_ostentatious_overseers_mod_effect
		hidden_effect = {
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = slaves
				}
				add_province_modifier = {
					name = estate_nobles_orldhum_ostentatious_overseers_mod
					duration = -1
				}
			}
		}
	}
	on_granted_province = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				trade_goods = slaves
			}
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = estate_nobles_orldhum_ostentatious_overseers_mod
				duration = -1
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_modifier = estate_nobles_orldhum_ostentatious_overseers_mod
			}
			remove_province_modifier = estate_nobles_orldhum_ostentatious_overseers_mod
		}
	}
	on_revoked_province = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_province_modifier = estate_nobles_orldhum_ostentatious_overseers_mod }
			remove_province_modifier = estate_nobles_orldhum_ostentatious_overseers_mod
		}
	}
	on_invalid_province = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_province_modifier = estate_nobles_orldhum_ostentatious_overseers_mod }
			remove_province_modifier = estate_nobles_orldhum_ostentatious_overseers_mod
		}
	}
	penalties = {
	}
	benefits = {
	}
	conditional_modifier = {
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				estate_loyalty = {
					estate = estate_nobles
					loyalty = 30
				}
			}
			NOT = { has_country_flag = orldhum_legit }
		}
		modifier = {
			production_efficiency = -0.2
		}
		is_bad = yes
	}
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 5
	}
}

	icon = privilege_monopoly_of_goods_slaves
	max_absolutism = -10
	conditional_modifier = { trigger = { has_absolutism_reduction_for_estate_privileges = yes } modifier = { max_absolutism = 2 } }
	loyalty = 0.15
	influence = 0.1
	is_valid = {
		has_country_flag = G53_independent_trading_unlocked_flag
		any_owned_province = {
			trade_goods = slaves
		}
	}
	can_select = {
	}
	on_granted = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				slaves = 1
			}
			add_mercantilism = 1
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = empkeios_events.1200
			}
		}
		custom_tooltip = empkeios_slaveIncome_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = empkeios_events.2603
				days = 1
			}
		}
	}
	on_granted_province = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				trade_goods = slaves
			}
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = estate_burghers_slaver_independent_trading_mod
				duration = -1
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_modifier = estate_burghers_slaver_independent_trading_mod
			}
			remove_province_modifier = estate_burghers_slaver_independent_trading_mod
		}
	}
	on_revoked = {
		custom_tooltip = estate_burghers_empkeios_independent_trading_revoke_tt
	}
	on_revoked_province = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_modifier = estate_burghers_slaver_independent_trading_mod
			}
			remove_province_modifier = estate_burghers_slaver_independent_trading_mod
		}
	}
	on_invalid = {
		custom_tooltip = estate_burghers_empkeios_independent_trading_revoke_tt
	}
	on_invalid_province = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_modifier = estate_burghers_slaver_independent_trading_mod
			}
			remove_province_modifier = estate_burghers_slaver_independent_trading_mod
		}
	}
	penalties = {
	}
	benefits = {
	}

	cooldown_years = 10 
	conditional_modifier = {
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = buffed_monopolies
		}
		modifier = {
			burghers_privilege_slots = 1
		}
	}
	on_cooldown_expires = {
		country_event = { id = empkeios_events.2602 }
	}

		factor = 0
	}

estate_burghers_multiracial_crop_rotation = {
	icon = privilege_dev_cost
	
	influence = 0.1
	is_valid = { has_country_flag = unlocked_estate_burghers_multiracial_crop_rotation }
	can_select = { always = yes }
	can_revoke = {  always = yes }

	on_granted = {
		custom_tooltip = estate_burghers_multiracial_crop_rotation_tooltip
	}

	on_granted_province = {
		if = {
			limit = { OR = { trade_goods = serpentbloom trade_goods = fungi } }
			add_province_modifier = { name = skewered_drake_crop_caves duration = -1 hidden = yes }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { OR = { trade_goods = grain trade_goods = livestock } }
			add_province_modifier = { name = skewered_drake_crop_other duration = -1 hidden = yes }
		}
	}

	on_revoked_province = {
		remove_province_modifier = skewered_drake_crop_caves
		remove_province_modifier = skewered_drake_crop_other
	}

	benefits = {
		global_unrest = -1
	}

	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 100
	}
}

estate_church_sand_molding = {
	icon = privilege_dev_cost_desert
	max_absolutism = -10
	land_share = 5
	conditional_modifier = { trigger = { has_country_flag = estate_church_no_absolutism_cost } modifier = { max_absolutism = 10 } }
	conditional_modifier = { trigger = { has_absolutism_reduction_for_estate_privileges = yes NOT = { has_country_flag = estate_church_no_absolutism_cost } } modifier = { max_absolutism = 2 } }
	influence = 0.10
	loyalty = 0.10
	is_valid = {
		has_unlocked_estate_privilege = { estate_privilege = estate_church_sand_molding }
	}
	can_select = {
		any_owned_province = {
			OR = {
				has_terrain = desert
				has_terrain = coastal_desert
			}
		}
	}
	on_granted = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = irkorzik_upgraded_sand_molding_2
			}
			custom_tooltip = estate_church_sand_molding_gt_2
		}
		else = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = irkorzik_upgraded_sand_molding_1
				}
				custom_tooltip = estate_church_sand_molding_gt_1
			}
			else = {
				custom_tooltip = estate_church_sand_molding_gt
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = irkorzik_upgraded_sand_molding_2
				}
				every_owned_province = {
					limit = {
						has_terrain = desert
					}
					add_province_modifier = {
						name = irkorzik_sand_molding_super_desert
						duration = -1
					}
				}
				every_owned_province = {
					limit = {
						has_terrain = coastal_desert
					}
					add_province_modifier = {
						name = irkorzik_sand_molding_super_coastal_desert
						duration = -1
					}
				}	
			}	
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = irkorzik_upgraded_sand_molding_1
				}
				every_owned_province = {
					limit = {
						has_terrain = desert
					}
					add_province_modifier = {
						name = irkorzik_sand_molding_big_desert
						duration = -1
					}
				}
				every_owned_province = {
					limit = {
						has_terrain = coastal_desert
					}
					add_province_modifier = {
						name = irkorzik_sand_molding_big_coastal_desert
						duration = -1
					}
				}	
			}	
			else = {
				every_owned_province = {
					limit = {
						has_terrain = desert
					}
					add_province_modifier = {
						name = irkorzik_sand_molding_little_desert
						duration = -1
					}
				}
				every_owned_province = {
					limit = {
						has_terrain = coastal_desert
					}
					add_province_modifier = {
						name = irkorzik_sand_molding_little_coastal_desert
						duration = -1
					}
				}	
			}
		}
	}
	on_revoked = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = irkorzik_upgraded_sand_molding_2
			}
			custom_tooltip = estate_church_sand_molding_rt_2
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = irkorzik_upgraded_sand_molding_1
			}
			custom_tooltip = estate_church_sand_molding_rt_1
		}
		else = {
			custom_tooltip = estate_church_sand_molding_rt
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_province_modifier = irkorzik_sand_molding_little_desert
						has_province_modifier = irkorzik_sand_molding_little_coastal_desert
						has_province_modifier = irkorzik_sand_molding_big_desert
						has_province_modifier = irkorzik_sand_molding_big_coastal_desert
						has_province_modifier = irkorzik_sand_molding_super_desert
						has_province_modifier = irkorzik_sand_molding_super_coastal_desert
					}
				}
				remove_province_modifier = irkorzik_sand_molding_little_desert
				remove_province_modifier = irkorzik_sand_molding_little_coastal_desert
				remove_province_modifier = irkorzik_sand_molding_big_desert
				remove_province_modifier = irkorzik_sand_molding_big_coastal_desert
				remove_province_modifier = irkorzik_sand_molding_super_desert
				remove_province_modifier = irkorzik_sand_molding_super_coastal_desert
			}
		}
	}
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 100
	}
}

estate_church_sandstorm_summoning = {
	icon = privilege_dev_cost_desert
	influence = 0.10
	loyalty = 0.05
	is_valid = {
		has_unlocked_estate_privilege = { estate_privilege = estate_church_sandstorm_summoning }
	}
	can_select = {  }
	benefits = {
		church_privilege_slots = 1
	}
	on_granted = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = irkorzik_upgraded_sandstorm_summoning
			}
			custom_tooltip = estate_church_sandstorm_summoning_buff_gt
		}
		else = {
			custom_tooltip = estate_church_sandstorm_summoning_gt
		}
	}
	on_granted_province = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				AND = {
					owner = { has_country_flag = irkorzik_upgraded_sandstorm_summoning }
					NOT = { has_province_modifier = irkorzik_sandstorm_wall }
					NOT = { has_province_modifier = irkorzik_sandstorm_wall_buff }
					has_building = mage_tower
				}
			}
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = irkorzik_sandstorm_summoning_buff
				duration = -1
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				AND = {
					has_building = mage_tower
					NOT = { has_province_modifier = irkorzik_sandstorm_wall }
					NOT = { has_province_modifier = irkorzik_sandstorm_wall_buff }
				}
			}
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = irkorzik_sandstorm_summoning
				duration = -1
			}
		}
	}
	on_invalid_province = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_province_modifier = irkorzik_sandstorm_summoning }
			remove_province_modifier = irkorzik_sandstorm_summoning
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_province_modifier = irkorzik_sandstorm_summoning_buff }
			remove_province_modifier = irkorzik_sandstorm_summoning_buff
		}
	}
	on_revoked_province = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_province_modifier = irkorzik_sandstorm_summoning }
			remove_province_modifier = irkorzik_sandstorm_summoning
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_province_modifier = irkorzik_sandstorm_summoning_buff }
			remove_province_modifier = irkorzik_sandstorm_summoning_buff
		}
	}
	on_revoked = {
		custom_tooltip = estate_church_sandstorm_summoning_buff_rt
	}
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 100
	}
}

#Exwes
estate_burghers_exwes_leading_naval_supplier = {
	icon = privilege_ducats
	land_share = 5
	max_absolutism = -10
	conditional_modifier = { trigger = { has_absolutism_reduction_for_estate_privileges = yes } modifier = { max_absolutism = 2 } }
	influence = 0.05
	loyalty = 0.05
	is_valid = {
		has_unlocked_estate_privilege = { estate_privilege = estate_burghers_exwes_leading_naval_supplier }
		has_estate = estate_burghers
	}
	can_select = {
		has_estate = estate_burghers
	}
	can_revoke = {
		estate_loyalty = {
			estate = estate_burghers
			higher_than_influence = yes
		}
	}
	on_granted = {
		custom_tooltip = estate_burghers_exwes_leading_naval_supplier_effect_tt
	}
	on_granted_province = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_wharf_trade_goods = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_building = impressment_offices
						has_building = wharf
					}
				}
				add_province_modifier = {
					name = burghers_estate_exwes_wharf_trade_up
					duration = -1
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_modifier = burghers_estate_exwes_wharf_trade_up
			}
			remove_province_modifier = burghers_estate_exwes_wharf_trade_up
		}
	}
	on_revoked = {
		custom_tooltip = estate_burghers_exwes_leading_naval_supplier_revoke_effect_tt
		add_estate_loyalty = {
			estate = estate_burghers
			loyalty = -20
		}
	}
	on_revoked_province = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_modifier = burghers_estate_exwes_wharf_trade_up
			}
			remove_province_modifier = burghers_estate_exwes_wharf_trade_up
		}
	}
	on_invalid = {
		custom_tooltip = estate_burghers_exwes_leading_naval_supplier_revoke_effect_tt
	}
	on_invalid_province = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_modifier = burghers_estate_exwes_wharf_trade_up
			}
			remove_province_modifier = burghers_estate_exwes_wharf_trade_up
		}
	}
	penalties = {
	}
	benefits = {
	}
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 100
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			num_of_owned_provinces_with = {
				AND = {
					has_wharf_trade_goods = yes
					OR = {
						has_building = wharf
						has_building = impressment_offices
					}
				}
				value = 5
			}
		}
	}
}

	can_revoke = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = L68_choose_sack
			}
			treasury = 800
		}
		else = {
			treasury = 1000
		}	
	}
	on_revoked = {
		if = {
			limit = {  
				NOT = { has_country_flag = L68_choose_sack }
			}
			add_treasury = -1000
		}
		else = {
			add_treasury = -800
		} 
		reduce_estate_burghers_loyalty_effect = yes
	}
	penalties = {
		interest = 1
		trade_efficiency = -0.1
	}
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = -300
	}
}

#Lizardfolk - Mutation Privileges

estate_church_naga_mutation = {
	icon = privilege_lizardfolk_mutation
	max_absolutism = -10
	conditional_modifier = { trigger = { mission_completed = khatalashya_two_hubs_of_naga } modifier = { max_absolutism = 30 } }
	conditional_modifier = { trigger = { has_country_flag = estate_church_no_absolutism_cost NOT = { mission_completed = khatalashya_two_hubs_of_naga } } modifier = { max_absolutism = 10 } }
	conditional_modifier = { trigger = { has_absolutism_reduction_for_estate_privileges = yes NOT = { has_country_flag = estate_church_no_absolutism_cost mission_completed = khatalashya_two_hubs_of_naga } } modifier = { max_absolutism = 2 } }
	loyalty = 0.05
	influence = 0.1
	is_valid = { 
		culture_is_lizardfolk = yes
		religion = anzalkatsa
		NOT = { has_country_flag = rayaz_naga_upgraded }
		NOT = { has_country_flag = nagas_forbidden }
		NOT = {
			has_estate_privilege = estate_church_struggle_against_nagas
		}
		NOT = {
			has_estate_privilege = estate_church_state_loyal_nagas
		}
		NOT = {
			overlord = {
				has_estate_privilege = estate_church_struggle_against_nagas
			}
		}
		NOT = {
			overlord = {
				has_estate_privilege = estate_church_state_loyal_nagas
			}
		}
	}
	can_select = {
		NOT = {
			AND = {
				has_estate_privilege = estate_church_abundance_of_nagas_mutation
				has_estate_privilege = estate_church_naga_upgraded_mutation
			}
		}
		NOT = {
			has_estate_privilege = estate_nobles_nobility_primacy
		}
		can_have_more_mutations = yes
	}
	on_granted = {
		khatalashya_add_debuff_hive_privilage = { mutation = naga }
	}
	can_revoke = {
		estate_has_stability_to_revoke_mutation = { 2 = yes }
	}
	on_revoked = {
		estate_remove_stability_when_revoke_mutation = { 3 = yes }
		khatalashya_loyalty_on_revokation_church = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_disaster = the_hivemind
				has_country_flag = the_hivemind_naga_ap
			}
			khatalashya_remove_debuff_hive_main = { mutation = naga }
		}
	}
	on_invalid = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_disaster = the_hivemind
				has_country_flag = the_hivemind_naga_ap
			}
			khatalashya_remove_debuff_hive_main = { mutation = naga }
		}
	}
	penalties = {
		technology_cost = 0.05
		stability_cost_modifier = 0.15
	}
	benefits = {
		tolerance_own = 1
		all_power_cost = -0.025
	}
	conditional_modifier = {
		trigger = {
			mission_completed = khatalashya_investigate_every_lizard
		}
		modifier = {
			governing_capacity = 25
		}
	}
	conditional_modifier = {
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = naga_no_stability_cost
		} 
		modifier = {
			stability_cost_modifier = -0.15
		}
	}
	conditional_modifier = {
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = naga_no_technology_cost
		}
		modifier = {
			technology_cost = -0.05
		}
	}
	conditional_modifier = {
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = L68_no_naga 
		}
		modifier = {
			church_loyalty_modifier = -0.05
		}
	}
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 10
	}
}

#Mutations for Asarta

estate_church_akhaxpa_mutation = {
	icon = privilege_lizardfolk_mutation
	land_share = 0
	max_absolutism = -10
	conditional_modifier = { trigger = { has_country_flag = estate_church_no_absolutism_cost } modifier = { max_absolutism = 10 } }
	conditional_modifier = { trigger = { has_absolutism_reduction_for_estate_privileges = yes NOT = { has_country_flag = estate_church_no_absolutism_cost } } modifier = { max_absolutism = 2 } }
	loyalty = -0.05
	influence = 0.1
	is_valid = {
		has_country_flag = asarta_mutation_tier1
	}
	can_select = {
		can_have_more_mutations = yes
	}
	can_revoke = {
		stability = 2
	}
	on_granted = {
		custom_tooltip = akhaxpa_akhaxazai_tt
		khatalashya_add_debuff_hive_privilage = { mutation = akhaxazai }
	}
	on_revoked = {
		add_stability = -2
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					estate_loyalty = {
					estate = estate_church
					loyalty = 60
					}
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = asarta_change_is_coming_tt
			decrease_ruler_adm_effect = yes
			decrease_ruler_dip_effect = yes
			decrease_ruler_mil_effect = yes
		}
		khatalashya_loyalty_on_revokation_church = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_disaster = the_hivemind
				has_country_flag = the_hivemind_akhaxazai_ap
			}
			khatalashya_remove_debuff_hive_main = { mutation = akhaxazai }
		}
	}
	on_invalid = {
		if = {

		}

			}

		}

		custom_tooltip = estate_church_spring_tolerance_revoke_effect_tooltip

				has_province_modifier = estate_church_spring_tolerance_mod

estate_church_autumn_tolerance = {
	icon = privilege_grant_autonomy
	max_absolutism = -5
	conditional_modifier = { trigger = { has_country_flag = estate_church_no_absolutism_cost } modifier = { max_absolutism = 5 } }
	conditional_modifier = { trigger = { has_absolutism_reduction_for_estate_privileges = yes NOT = { has_country_flag = estate_church_no_absolutism_cost } } modifier = { max_absolutism = 1 } }
	influence = 0.05
	loyalty = -0.05
	is_valid = {
		religion = autumn_court
	}
	can_select = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_reform = raithtall_twilight_court_reform }
			OR = {
				has_reform = raithtall_twilight_court_reform
				num_of_owned_provinces_with = {
					value = 4
					OR = {
						religion = spring_court
						religion = summer_court
					}
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			num_of_owned_provinces_with = {
				value = 4
				OR = {
					religion = spring_court
					religion = summer_court
				}
			}
		}
	}
	on_granted = {
		custom_tooltip = estate_church_autumn_tolerance_effect_tooltip
	}
	on_granted_province = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					religion = spring_court
					religion = summer_court
				}
			}
			#Raithtall privilege upgrade
			if = {
				limit = { owner = { has_country_flag = raithtall_autumn_tolerance } }
				add_province_modifier = {
					name = estate_church_autumn_tolerance_mod_upgraded
					duration = -1
				}
			}
			else = {
				add_province_modifier = {
					name = estate_church_autumn_tolerance_mod
					duration = -1
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_province_modifier = estate_church_autumn_tolerance_mod
					has_province_modifier = estate_church_autumn_tolerance_mod_upgraded
				}
			}
			remove_province_modifier = estate_church_autumn_tolerance_mod
			remove_province_modifier = estate_church_autumn_tolerance_mod_upgraded
		}
	}
	can_revoke = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_reform = raithtall_twilight_court_reform }
			NOT = { has_reform = raithtall_twilight_court_reform }
		}
	}
	on_revoked = {
		custom_tooltip = estate_church_autumn_tolerance_revoke_effect_tooltip
	}
	on_revoked_province = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_modifier = estate_church_autumn_tolerance_mod
			}
			remove_province_modifier = estate_church_autumn_tolerance_mod
		}
	}
	on_invalid = {
		custom_tooltip = estate_church_autumn_tolerance_revoke_effect_tooltip
	}
	on_invalid_province = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_modifier = estate_church_autumn_tolerance_mod
			}
			remove_province_modifier = estate_church_autumn_tolerance_mod
		}
	}
	penalties = {
	}
	benefits = {
	}
	influence_scaled_conditional_modifier = {	#Modifier that are applied if the specified conditions are true. At 100% Influence you gain 100% of the modifier.
		modifier = { manpower_in_true_faith_provinces = 0.2 }
	}
	ai_will_do = { factor = 0 }
}

estate_noble_monopoly_of_fuel = {
	icon = privilege_monopoly_of_goods_cloth
	loyalty = 0.05
	is_valid = {
		OR = {
			has_dlc = "Emperor"
			has_country_flag = buffed_monopolies
		}
		any_owned_province = {
			trade_goods = tropical_wood
		}
		has_country_flag = karakhanbar_monopoly_on_fuel
	}
	can_select = {
		custom_trigger_tooltip = {
			tooltip = unavailable_during_revolution_disaster
			NOT = { has_disaster = revolution }
			NOT = {
				has_disaster_progress = {
					disaster = revolution
					value = 1
				}
			}
		}
	}
	on_granted = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				tropical_wood = 1
			}
			add_mercantilism = 1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = karakhanbar_upgrade_of_monopoly
			}
			add_years_of_owned_provinces_production_income = {
				years = 12
				trigger = {
					trade_goods = tropical_wood
				}
				custom_tooltip = MONOPOLY_INCOME_TROPICAL_WOOD_DESC
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_years_of_owned_provinces_production_income = {
				years = 8
				trigger = {
					trade_goods = tropical_wood
				}
				custom_tooltip = MONOPOLY_INCOME_TROPICAL_WOOD_DESC
			}
		}
	}
	on_granted_province = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				trade_goods = tropical_wood
			}
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = estate_noble_monopoly_of_fuel_mod
				duration = -1
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_modifier = estate_noble_monopoly_of_fuel_mod
			}
			remove_province_modifier = estate_noble_monopoly_of_fuel_mod
		}
	}
	on_revoked = { }
	on_revoked_province = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_modifier = estate_noble_monopoly_of_fuel_mod
			}
			remove_province_modifier = estate_noble_monopoly_of_fuel_mod
		}
	}
	on_invalid = { }
	on_invalid_province = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_modifier = estate_noble_monopoly_of_fuel_mod
			}
			remove_province_modifier = estate_noble_monopoly_of_fuel_mod
		}
	}
	penalties = {
	}
	benefits = {
		monthly_karakhanbar_flames_of_the_black_hearth_power = 0.5
	}
	cooldown_years = 10
	on_cooldown_expires = {
		country_event = { id = monopoly_privileges.20 }
	}
	ai_will_do = { #having the AI use these could lead to an unstoppable downwards spiral if it can't work out how to get rid of them
		factor = 0
	}
}

				tag = Z99
				was_tag = B39
			}
		}
	}
	can_select = { mission_completed = the_hearter_homeland }
	on_granted = {
		custom_tooltip = estate_wyvernheart_culture_of_the_heart_tta
		custom_tooltip = estate_wyvernheart_culture_of_the_heart_ttb
	}
	on_granted_province = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				culture = ROOT
			}
			remove_province_modifier = estate_wyvernheart_culture_of_the_heart_weak_culture_mod
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = estate_wyvernheart_culture_of_the_heart_mod
				duration = -1
			}
		}
		else = {
			remove_province_modifier = estate_wyvernheart_culture_of_the_heart_mod
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = estate_wyvernheart_culture_of_the_heart_weak_culture_mod
				duration = -1
			}
		}
	}
	on_revoked = {
		custom_tooltip = estate_wyvernheart_culture_of_the_heart_rta
		custom_tooltip = estate_wyvernheart_culture_of_the_heart_rtb
	}
	on_revoked_province = {
	}
	on_invalid = {
	}
	on_invalid_province = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				culture = ROOT
			}
			remove_province_modifier = estate_wyvernheart_culture_of_the_heart_mod
		}
		else = {
			remove_province_modifier = estate_wyvernheart_culture_of_the_heart_weak_culture_mod
		}
	}
	penalties = {
		tolerance_heathen = -2
		tolerance_heretic = -2
	}
	benefits = {
		global_missionary_strength = 0.01
	}
	can_revoke = {
		always = no
	}
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 1
	}
}

estate_burghers_gnollish_crafters = {
	icon = privilege_artificers_development_tools
	loyalty = 0.10
	influence = 0.10
	
	is_valid = { 
		has_country_flag = s23_gnollish_crafters_unlock 
		NOT = { has_estate_privilege = estate_burghers_gnollish_crafters_bad }
	}
	can_select = { has_country_flag = s23_gnollish_crafters_unlock  }
	can_revoke = { always = yes }

	on_granted = {
		custom_tooltip = s23_gnollish_crafters_tt
	}
	on_granted_province = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_gnollish_majority_trigger = yes
			}
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = s23_big_gnoll
				duration = -1
			}
			remove_province_modifier = s23_smol_gnoll
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { 
				has_gnollish_minority_trigger = yes
			}
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = s23_smol_gnoll
				duration = -1
			}
			remove_province_modifier = s23_big_gnoll
		}
		else = {
			remove_province_modifier = s23_big_gnoll
			remove_province_modifier = s23_smol_gnoll
		}
    }
	on_revoked = {
	}
	on_revoked_province = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_modifier = s23_big_gnoll
			}
			remove_province_modifier = s23_big_gnoll
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_modifier = s23_smol_gnoll
			}
			remove_province_modifier = s23_smol_gnoll
		}
	}
	on_invalid = {
	}
	on_invalid_province = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_modifier = s23_big_gnoll
			}
			remove_province_modifier = s23_big_gnoll
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_modifier = s23_smol_gnoll
			}
			remove_province_modifier = s23_smol_gnoll
		}
	}

	penalties = {
	}

	benefits = {
	}
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 1000
	}
}

estate_adventurers_rangers_ayeth_strategy = {
	icon = privilege_land_rights
	loyalty = 0.05
	influence = 0.1
	max_absolutism = -5
	conditional_modifier = { trigger = { has_absolutism_reduction_for_estate_privileges = yes } modifier = { max_absolutism = 1 } }
	is_valid = { 
		primary_culture = wood_elf
		NOT = { has_country_flag = deepwoods_rangers_disabled }
	}
	can_select = {
		any_owned_province = {
			has_province_modifier = deepwoods_rangers_camp
		}
		custom_trigger_tooltip = {
			tooltip = deepwoods_ranger_strategy_cooldown
			OR = {
				NOT = { has_country_flag = picked_ranger_strategy_privilege }
				had_country_flag = {
					flag = picked_ranger_strategy_privilege
					days = 3650
				}
			}
		}
	}
	on_granted = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_estate_privilege = estate_adventurers_rangers_scotha_strategy }
			remove_estate_privilege = estate_adventurers_rangers_scotha_strategy
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_estate_privilege = estate_mages_rangers_drennen_strategy }
			remove_estate_privilege = estate_mages_rangers_drennen_strategy
		}
		custom_tooltip = deepwoods_rangers_ayeth_strategy_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = { has_province_modifier = deepwoods_rangers_camp }
				add_province_modifier = {
					name = deepwoods_rangers_ayeth_strategy_mod
					duration = -1
				}
				every_neighbor_province = {
					limit = { owned_by = ROOT }
					add_province_modifier = {
						name = deepwoods_rangers_ayeth_strategy_mod
						duration = -1
					}
				}
			}
			clr_country_flag = picked_ranger_strategy_privilege
			set_country_flag = picked_ranger_strategy_privilege
		}
	}
	on_revoked = {
		every_owned_province = {
			remove_province_modifier = deepwoods_rangers_ayeth_strategy_mod
		}
	}
	cooldown_years = 10
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 1
	}
}

estate_burghers_committe_of_urban_development = {
	icon = privilege_development_efficiency
	max_absolutism = -10
	conditional_modifier = { trigger = { has_absolutism_reduction_for_estate_privileges = yes } modifier = { max_absolutism = 2 } }
	loyalty = 0.1
	influence = 0.1
	land_share = 0
	is_valid = {
		has_country_flag = pashaine_enable_urban_privilege
	}
	can_revoke = { always = yes }

	on_granted = {
		custom_tooltip = estate_burghers_committe_of_urban_development_grant_tt
		tooltip = {
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = pashaine_urban_development
				duration = -1
			}
		}
		remove_estate_privilege = estate_burghers_development_of_cities
		remove_estate_privilege = estate_burghers_exclusive_trade_rights
	}
	on_revoked = {
		custom_tooltip = estate_burghers_committe_of_urban_development_removed_tt
	}

	on_granted_province = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_terrain = city_terrain
					province_has_center_of_trade_of_level = 1
					has_river_estuary_trigger = yes
				}
			}
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = pashaine_urban_development
				duration = -1
			}
		}
	}

	on_invalid_province = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_province_modifier = pashaine_urban_development }
			remove_province_modifier = pashaine_urban_development
		}
	}

	on_revoked_province = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_province_modifier = pashaine_urban_development }
			remove_province_modifier = pashaine_urban_development
		}
	}
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 1
	}
}

		remove_province_modifier = z22_commercial_language_notblue_2

		}

	}

estate_monstrous_tribes_supplement_levies = {
	icon = privilege_one_faith_one_culture
	influence = -0.05
	loyalty = 0.05
	is_valid = {
		religion = shadow_pact
	}
	can_select = {
		has_country_flag = shadow_warriors_levies_1
	}
	on_granted = {
		add_corruption = 1
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = shadow_warriors_levies_2_2 }
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = shadow_warriors_levies_2_2
				duration = -1
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = shadow_warriors_levies_2_1 }
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = shadow_warriors_levies_2_1
				duration = -1
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = shadow_warriors_levies_1
				duration = -1
			}
		}
	}
	on_granted_province = {
	}
	on_revoked = {
		remove_country_modifier = shadow_warriors_levies_1
		remove_country_modifier = shadow_warriors_levies_2_1
		remove_country_modifier = shadow_warriors_levies_2_2
	}
	on_revoked_province = {
	}
	on_invalid = {
	}
	on_invalid_province = {
	}
	penalties = {
		yearly_corruption = 0.1
	}
	benefits = {
	}
	conditional_modifier = {
		trigger = { has_country_flag = shadow_warriors_levies_2_1 }
		modifier = {
			stability_cost_modifier = -0.15
		}
	}
	conditional_modifier = {
		trigger = { has_country_flag = shadow_warriors_levies_2_2 }
		modifier = {
			global_unrest = 2
		}
	}
	cooldown_years = 10
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 10
#		modifier = {
#			factor = 0
#			
#		}
	}
}


#karassk stuff
estate_burghers_khair_families_our_land = {
	icon = privilege_recruit_minister
	influence = 0.05
	loyalty = 0.05
	is_valid = { 
		has_country_flag = L68_our_land_unlock
	}
	can_select = {
		has_country_flag = L68_our_land_unlock
	}
	can_revoke = {
		always = no
	}
	on_granted = {
		custom_tooltip = estate_burghers_khair_families_our_land_non_cult_tt
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = L68_our_land_cult_upg
			}
			custom_tooltip = estate_burghers_khair_families_our_land_cult_tt
		}
	}
	on_granted_province = {
		if = {
			limit = { fast_has_pop_of_race = { race = human } }

			if = {
				limit = {
					has_port = yes
					has_human_minority_trigger = yes
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						owner = {
							medium_tolerance_human_race_trigger = yes
						}
					}
					add_province_modifier = { name = L68_khair_families_our_land_goods_co duration = -1 }
					remove_province_modifier = L68_khair_families_our_land_goods_notco
				}
				else = {
					add_province_modifier = { name = L68_khair_families_our_land_goods_notco duration = -1 }
					remove_province_modifier = L68_khair_families_our_land_goods_co
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					owner = { has_country_flag = L68_our_land_cult_upg }
					has_human_majority_trigger = yes
				}
				
				if = {
					limit = {
						owner = {
							medium_tolerance_human_race_trigger = yes
						}
					}
					add_province_modifier = { name = L68_khair_families_our_land_cult_co duration = -1 }
					remove_province_modifier = L68_khair_families_our_land_cult_notco
				}
				else = {
					add_province_modifier = { name = L68_khair_families_our_land_cult_notco duration = -1 }
					remove_province_modifier = L68_khair_families_our_land_cult_co
				}
					
			}
		}
	}
	
	on_revoked = {
		custom_tooltip = estate_burghers_khair_families_our_land_non_cult_tt
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = L68_our_land_cult_upg
			}
			custom_tooltip = estate_burghers_khair_families_our_land_cult_tt
		}
	}

	on_revoked_province = {
		remove_province_modifier = L68_khair_families_our_land_goods_co
		remove_province_modifier = L68_khair_families_our_land_goods_notco
		remove_province_modifier = L68_khair_families_our_land_cult_co
		remove_province_modifier = L68_khair_families_our_land_cult_notco
	}
	on_invalid = {
	}
	on_invalid_province = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_province_modifier = L68_khair_families_our_land_goods_co
					has_province_modifier = L68_khair_families_our_land_goods_notco
					has_province_modifier = L68_khair_families_our_land_cult_co
					has_province_modifier = L68_khair_families_our_land_cult_notco
				}
			}
			remove_province_modifier = L68_khair_families_our_land_goods_co
			remove_province_modifier = L68_khair_families_our_land_goods_notco
			remove_province_modifier = L68_khair_families_our_land_cult_co
			remove_province_modifier = L68_khair_families_our_land_cult_notco
		}
	}
	penalties = {
		yearly_corruption = 0.05
	}
	benefits = {
		burghers_privilege_slots = 1
	}
	
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 10
	}
}

estate_burghers_khair_families_the_right_to_teach = {
	icon = privilege_recruit_minister
	influence = 0.05
	loyalty = 0.05
	is_valid = {

	}

		always = no
	}

		set_country_flag = disabled_expelling_human_flag
		set_country_flag = disabled_purging_human_flag
		custom_tooltip = estate_burghers_khair_families_the_right_to_teach_tt
	}

	on_granted_province = {
		if = {
			limit = { fast_has_pop_of_race = { race = human } }

			if = {
				limit = {
					owner = {
						medium_tolerance_human_race_trigger = yes
					}
				}
				add_province_modifier = { name = L68_khair_families_right_to_teach_co duration = -1 }
				remove_province_modifier = L68_khair_families_right_to_teach_notco
			}
			else = {
				add_province_modifier = { name = L68_khair_families_right_to_teach_notco duration = -1 }
				remove_province_modifier = L68_khair_families_right_to_teach_co
			}
		}
		
	}
	
	on_revoked = {
		clr_country_flag = disabled_expelling_human_flag
		clr_country_flag = disabled_purging_human_flag
		custom_tooltip = estate_burghers_khair_families_the_right_to_teach_tt
	}

	on_revoked_province = {
		remove_province_modifier = L68_khair_families_right_to_teach_co
		remove_province_modifier = L68_khair_families_right_to_teach_notco
	}
	on_invalid = {
	}
	on_invalid_province = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_province_modifier = L68_khair_families_right_to_teach_co
					has_province_modifier = L68_khair_families_right_to_teach_notco
				}
			}
			remove_province_modifier = L68_khair_families_right_to_teach_co
			remove_province_modifier = L68_khair_families_right_to_teach_notco
		}
	}
	penalties = {
		yearly_corruption = 0.05
	}
	benefits = {
		promote_culture_cost = -0.25
		burghers_privilege_slots = 1
	}
	
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 10
	}
}

	on_granted_province = {
		if = {
			limit = { fast_has_pop_of_race = { race = human } }

			if = {
				limit = {
					owner = {
						medium_tolerance_human_race_trigger = yes
					}
				}
				add_province_modifier = { name = L68_khair_families_iysashlagila_management_lanforce_co duration = -1 }
				remove_province_modifier = L68_khair_families_iysashlagila_management_lanforce_notco
			}
			else = {
				add_province_modifier = { name = L68_khair_families_iysashlagila_management_lanforce_notco duration = -1 }
				remove_province_modifier = L68_khair_families_iysashlagila_management_lanforce_co
			}

			if = {
				limit = { has_human_majority_trigger = yes }
				add_province_modifier = { name = L68_khair_families_iysashlagila_management_maj_man_debuff duration = -1 }
			}
		}
	}
	
	on_revoked = {
		custom_tooltip = estate_burghers_khair_families_iysashlagila_management_tt
	}

	on_revoked_province = {
		remove_province_modifier = L68_khair_families_iysashlagila_management_lanforce_co
		remove_province_modifier = L68_khair_families_iysashlagila_management_lanforce_notco
		remove_province_modifier = L68_khair_families_iysashlagila_management_maj_man_debuff
	}
	on_invalid = {
	}
	on_invalid_province = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_province_modifier = L68_khair_families_iysashlagila_management_lanforce_co
					has_province_modifier = L68_khair_families_iysashlagila_management_lanforce_notco
					has_province_modifier = L68_khair_families_iysashlagila_management_maj_man_debuff
				}
			}
			remove_province_modifier = L68_khair_families_iysashlagila_management_lanforce_co
			remove_province_modifier = L68_khair_families_iysashlagila_management_lanforce_notco
			remove_province_modifier = L68_khair_families_iysashlagila_management_maj_man_debuff
		}
	}
	penalties = {
		yearly_corruption = 0.05
	}
	benefits = {
		mercenary_manpower = 0.20
		mercenary_discipline = 0.025 
		mercenary_cost = -0.1
		burghers_privilege_slots = 1
	}
	
	conditional_modifier = {

			medium_tolerance_human_race_trigger = yes
		}
		modifier = {

		}

estate_nobles_monopoly_of_exotic_wood = {
	icon = privilege_monopoly
	max_absolutism = -10
	conditional_modifier = { trigger = { has_absolutism_reduction_for_estate_privileges = yes } modifier = { max_absolutism = 2 } }
	loyalty = 0.05
	is_valid = {
		has_country_flag = karach_exotic_wood_monopoly
		OR = {
			has_dlc = "Emperor"
			has_country_flag = buffed_monopolies
		}
		tropical_wood = 1
	}
	can_select = {
		custom_trigger_tooltip = {
			tooltip = unavailable_during_revolution_disaster
			NOT = { has_disaster = revolution }
			NOT = {
				has_disaster_progress = {
					disaster = revolution
					value = 1
				}
			}
		}
		custom_trigger_tooltip = {
			tooltip = JY_LF_not_trading #Anbennar
			NOT = { has_country_modifier = JY_LF_recent_trade }
		}
	}
	on_granted = {
		add_mercantilism = 1
		add_years_of_owned_provinces_production_income = {
			years = 10
			trigger = {
				trade_goods = tropical_wood
			}
			custom_tooltip = MONOPOLY_INCOME_TROPICAL_WOOD_DESC
		}
		custom_tooltip = estate_nobles_monopoly_of_exotic_wood_effect_tooltip
	}
	on_granted_province = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				trade_goods = tropical_wood
			}
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = estate_nobles_monopoly_of_exotic_wood_mod
				duration = -1
			}
			if = {
				limit = { ROOT = { has_country_flag = karach_improved_nobles_monopolies_again } }
				add_province_modifier = {
					name = improved_province_monopoly_karach_nobles
					duration = -1
				}
			}
			else = {
				add_province_modifier = {
					name = improved_province_monopoly_karach
					duration = -1
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_modifier = estate_nobles_monopoly_of_exotic_wood_mod
			}
			remove_province_modifier = estate_nobles_monopoly_of_exotic_wood_mod
			remove_province_modifier = improved_province_monopoly_karach
			remove_province_modifier = improved_province_monopoly_karach_nobles
		}
	}
	on_revoked = {
		custom_tooltip = estate_nobles_monopoly_of_exotic_wood_revoke_tooltip
	}
	on_revoked_province = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_modifier = estate_nobles_monopoly_of_exotic_wood_mod
			}
			remove_province_modifier = estate_nobles_monopoly_of_exotic_wood_mod
		}
		remove_province_modifier = improved_province_monopoly_karach
		remove_province_modifier = improved_province_monopoly_karach_nobles
	}
	on_invalid = {
		custom_tooltip = estate_nobles_monopoly_of_exotic_wood_revoke_tooltip
	}
	on_invalid_province = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_modifier = estate_nobles_monopoly_of_exotic_wood_mod
			}
			remove_province_modifier = estate_nobles_monopoly_of_exotic_wood_mod
		}
		remove_province_modifier = improved_province_monopoly_karach
		remove_province_modifier = improved_province_monopoly_karach_nobles
	}
	penalties = {
	}
	benefits = {
	}
	cooldown_years = 10
	conditional_modifier = {
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = buffed_monopolies
		}
		modifier = {
			max_absolutism = 10
			nobles_privilege_slots = 1
		}
	}
	on_cooldown_expires = {
		country_event = { id = monopoly_privileges.21 }
	}
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 0
	}
